  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Comparative Advantage for Cookies and Brownies
  • QUESTION: The table below shows how long it takes two individuals, Amos and Debbi, to produce cookies and brownies. \r\n\r\n \r\n | |Amos | Debbi | \r\n |---|---|---| \r\n | Cookies | 1 hour | 2 hours | \r\n | Brownies | 2 hours | 3 hours | \r\n\r\n

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Comparative and Absolute Advantage for Authors
  • QUESTION: Scott can write $2$ novels or $20$ short stories each year. Ernest can write $1$ novel or $15$ short stories each year. Based on this information, which of the following is **TRUE**?
  • üòà ANSWER: C: Scott has the absolute advantage in writing both short stories and novels.

  • QUESTION: Which of the following must be true for trade to occur?
  • üòà ANSWER: A: Both parties must expect to benefit from the trade.

  • QUESTION: Which of the following market failures is a type of information asymmetry?

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Market Failure: Moral Hazard Definition
  • QUESTION: What is a moral hazard?
  • üòà ANSWER: A: The market failure that results from a change in the buyer\'s behavior after a purchase as a result of the buyer\'s belief that losses will be passed on to the seller.

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Description of Adverse Selection
  • QUESTION: Which of the following describes the market failure known as adverse selection?
  • üòà ANSWER: D: Parties to a transaction fear that there is negative information about the other party, or the goods or services, that they may not know.

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Inadequate Information about Potential Employees
  • QUESTION: Employers are sometimes hesitant to hire workers because they fear that the only potential employees that are currently looking for work are the least capable workers. This situation describes which of the following market failures?
  • üòà ANSWER: E: Adverse selection.

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Market Failure: New Restaurant
  • QUESTION: Sheldon refuses to eat at a new restaurant because he is concerned about whether the restaurant\'s employees have been properly trained concerning food safety. Which market failure does this represent?
  • üòà ANSWER: D: Information asymmetry

  • TITLE: AP Microeconomics - Identify Example of Information Asymmetry
  • QUESTION: Which of the following examples of market failures is the result of information asymmetry?
  • üòà ANSWER: E: A hospital produces less than the efficient quantity of medical services because some members of the community have doubts about the qualifications of the doctors and nurses.

  • üòà ANSWER: E: The choice of banks to make riskier loans after the FDIC begins to insure their deposits.

  • üòà ANSWER: D: Insurance companies may be reluctant to sell health insurance because they fear that only individuals with illnesses will buy it.
